Abolition of Change Fractions in Commercial Transactions

▲ The Money Trade Association Has Already Announced

The financial community proposed to abolish the change fractions of silver dollars in and out and to use fractions as the unit. The details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is understood that the Money Trade Association has announced the implementation of this matter, roughly saying that it was decided at the regular meeting on February 2nd of this year that the industry should use "li" as the unit for receiving and paying silver and silver dollars. Now, in order to facilitate calculation, the rounding method is used, and starting from February 16th of this year, all receipts and payments, whether silver or silver dollars, will be in units of "fen". Correspondingly, the record is notified, and you are requested to check and handle it. Yesterday's newspaper reported that it would start on February 19th, but the notice states that it would start on February 16th, because the 17th and 18th were the days when the silver and money industry settled the accounts for the 19th year and took a slight break.

Page 10

During the Account Closing Period, All Drafts Must Be Payable on Demand

For the convenience of commercial circulation of funds, money shops have long-term drafts with a ten-day term to replace cash. All commercial transactions are used as cash. Now that the money shop is in the period of closing the account for the 19th year, if long-term drafts are used again, they must be mixed with the business of the 20th year. In order to clearly define the boundaries, the committee has resolved that all merchants who want to issue drafts after February 15th should be limited to on-demand drafts and not issue long-term drafts. After this account closing period (that is, February 19th), the old rules will still be followed.

The Xin Kang Disaster Association is Actively Proceeding

▲ Eight Resolutions Passed

The Xin Kang Steamboat Disaster Family Association held a committee meeting yesterday afternoon to discuss the implementation methods. First, Committee Member Zhu reported that the negotiations with Japan on this case had not yielded results due to diplomatic methods, and there were many difficulties in the litigation process, resulting in the case being suspended for two years without a solution. The pain and reflection were inexplicable, and the indignation was unexplainable. Please discuss how to proceed. After the committee members successively expressed their opinions, they all said that the association should proceed with two points, internal and external. Externally, it should seek a quick resolution of the negotiations, and internally, it should seek the safety of the families. The colleagues of the association should work hard based on these two points and never give up. Secondly, it was resolved: (1) To send a telegram to the National Government, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, requesting that the rights of the country and the lives of the people be given priority and that serious negotiations be continued with the Japanese government, so as to ensure compensation for the loss of life and property; (2) To send a telegram to the whole country to carry out the abolition of all unequal treaties between China and Japan and to recover the right to navigate the territorial waters; (3) All committee members will go to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company on a regular basis to visit Director-General Li and ask him to announce the latest progress of the company's handling of the case and the definite direction of future negotiations; (4) In addition to the original legal counsel, Attorney Sheng Zhenwei, it is proposed to hire Attorney Wu Jingxiong as the legal counsel of the association, and Zhu and Zhou are publicly recommended to contact him; (5) The issue of relief for poor families, in addition to writing to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to consider ways to solve it, each committee member will also plan separately to fulfill the friendship of helping each other in the same boat; (6) The legal counsel is still requested to act as the full agent for the litigation and proceed effectively; (7) The issue of litigation expenses and relief will be directly requested by President Yang to understand the special circumstances and approve the relief; (8) Regularly go to the Japan Mail Steamship Company to visit the president of the company, give good-faith advice, and do not cover up the truth. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

The Collision Case Between the Yi Li and Chongqing Ships

▲ Arbitration Results

▲ Yi Li Does Not Accept

At 6:10 PM on March 28th of last year (the 19th year), the Yi Li ship of the Chinese Yi Li Shipping Company cast off its mooring cables from the Dada Wharf in Nanshi and set sail slowly downstream towards the Pudong side of the opposite bank. When passing the Lujiazui Water Police pontoon boat, the Chongqing ship of the British Taikoo Yangxing also approached the Pudong side and sailed upstream into the port. The Yi Li ship believed that the ship should not be sailing in this waterway, fearing a collision, and sounded its whistle once to make it pay attention to avoiding it. Unexpectedly, the ship answered with two whistles because it wanted to berth at the Pudong Wharf, indicating that it was unwilling to change course and still sailed straight towards the Yi Li ship. The Yi Li continued to sound its whistle three times, and reversed its engine and immediately dropped anchor, but the Chongqing ship also dropped anchor, but it still slammed into the Yi Li ship. At that time, the Yi Li ship was seriously injured, with repair costs estimated at more than 19,000 taels of silver. The Chongqing ship suffered only minor damage and left the port as usual. Afterwards, the Yi Li company issued a list to the Taikoo Yangxing, requesting compensation for the repair costs of more than 19,000 taels of silver, but the company refused to compensate. The Yi Li company originally intended to sue in court, but since the British consular jurisdiction in China has not yet been effectively abolished, it must file a lawsuit directly in its Shanghai court. However, according to past events, Chinese people suing foreign courts have never been able to obtain a fair judgment, so it was forced to ask the Taikoo Yangxing to ask a notary public to arbitrate and insisted on asking a person from a third country to serve as the arbitrator, but the Taikoo Yangxing still did not agree. After repeated negotiations, no results were obtained, so it was requested that the English port pilot Luo Shengzhelei (transliteration) of Songhu serve as the arbitrator. After the arbitration award was published, not only did Taikoo not compensate the Yi Li company for its losses, but it also wanted the Yi Li to compensate the Chongqing ship for repair costs of 4,000 yuan. Now the company has issued a letter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the Shipping Association, appealing to them to uphold justice and reassure our shipping industry. (Kwok Man Press)

Silk Factory Representatives Visit Zhang Shouyong Yesterday

▲ They Expressed Their Difficulties and Hoped for the Issuance of Silk Factory Public Bonds

The Shanghai Silk Factory Industry Association believes that the silk market in foreign firms is declining again, and the issuance of public bonds for the silk industry in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai is taking time. Each factory needs funds for relief, which is really urgent. A general meeting was convened the day before yesterday, and it was publicly decided to recommend representatives to petition Vice Minister Zhang Cai nearby. At 3:00 PM yesterday, the recommended representatives, such as Wang Xiaolai, Shen Huachen, Chu Huiseng, Huang Jin Chen, Shi Xinsheng, Huang Jinfan, Zhang Yunsheng, Wu Shenbo, Sun Rongchang, Yu Shouchang, Xu Yunjiang, Chen Mingshan, and other eleven people (Zhu Jing'an was absent due to business), gathered at the Beijing Road Weicheng Company and took cars to the Central Bank to visit Vice Minister Zhang Cai. They were received, and representatives such as Chu Huisheng, Shen Huachen, and Wang Xiaolai successively stated the difficult situation of the silk industry and said that the failure of silk factory operations last year almost led to total bankruptcy. Afterwards, the industry associations in the three regions of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai discussed and submitted a request to the government to issue public bonds for relief. Chairman Chiang and Ministers Song and Kong of the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry approved the issuance. Your Minister, the director in charge, came to Shanghai and convened a meeting of industry representatives to decide to issue 7 million yuan of public bonds, with 1 million yuan (later added another 1 million yuan) for improving sericulture and 6 million yuan for relieving silk factories in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai. The Executive Yuan, etc., have been requested to issue the bonds and are on file. Later, when the price of gold soared and the exchange rate fell, the sale of factory silk in Europe suddenly started, and Japanese merchants started buying to replenish their supplies. The market price of B-grade silk rose to more than 1,000 taels. The financial community believed that the issuance of public bonds was imminent and that they would be offset by something, so they lent the dried cocoons they had received as collateral to the factories to help them start work. Those who tried to start work in the past month only accounted for one-tenth of the total. However, it was a flash in the pan, and the sale of silk in Europe became sluggish again. The price of yarn fell sharply by more than 100 taels. According to the current cost of factory yarn, it cannot be maintained unless the price of silk reaches 1,300 taels. It is still necessary to lose more than 300 taels of silver per bale. Moreover, the account closing period is approaching, and the industry needs funds for turnover urgently. If the public bonds are not issued immediately, the silk factories that have not started will have no hope of recovery, and those that have started will also be unable to support themselves. The trend is getting worse day by day, and the environment is getting more dangerous day by day. It is necessary to announce the silk factory public bond case as soon as possible to save the situation and provide funds for regulation. Vice Minister Zhang said that the Ministry of Finance has completed all issuance procedures and is only waiting for the Executive Yuan to reply. Now it is only a matter of time. Since the silk industry is so urgent, he will try to forward the request to the Executive Yuan and announce it as soon as possible. First, a committee will be organized to handle registration matters, and the organizational regulations will be drafted by himself tomorrow and announced together with the Ministry of Industry. The representatives expressed their gratitude to Vice Minister Zhang and left.

Datong Music Society Rushes to Practice Six Chapters of Zhonghe Shao Music

▲ New Musical Instruments are Used for the Completion Ceremony

The Shanghai Datong Music Society has completed the construction of a complete set of ancient and modern musical instruments. The appearance is exquisite, and the content can be coordinated. It is planned to hold a completion ceremony in the near future, using all the newly built classical musical instruments to play Zhonghe Shao music, a total of six chapters: (1) Chapter of Taihe, (2) Chapter of Baohe, (3) Chapter of Xiehe, (4) Chapter of Xuanhe, (5) Chapter of Pinghe, (6) Chapter of Gonghe. Shao music was composed by Emperor Shun 4,000 years ago. Confucius called it perfect. Wu Jizha was amazed after watching the music. Qin Shihuang burned books and buried scholars alive, changing the established practices of the three dynasties. All kinds of music were abolished, but Shao music was specially preserved, which is enough to show the value of Shao music. From the Han Dynasty to the Qing Dynasty, the country used it for sacrifices to heaven and ancestors, and it was never changed. It is the origin of Chinese culture and the foundation of music, and it is the most credible of ancient music. Recently, in order to seek a fundamental solution, the association convened all the members of the large orchestra and worked hard to practice. The results have been very impressive. It is like entering a grand hall, as if in the bright sunshine, gentle breeze, and sweet rain, a scene of phoenixes singing and a dignified atmosphere, which makes people feel awed, leisurely thinking, and looking up high. Unknowingly, it reveals its inherent national character. At the beginning of the current hall, it is only a small part of the musical work, and the results have been very satisfactory. In the future, if we add banners, songs, and dances, and set up complete equipment, the results will be even more incredible.

Japanese Textile Merchants Establishing Factories in China

▲ Foreign Merchants Intensifying Competition

▲ Chinese Merchants Experiencing Increased Pressure

Since the price of gold became high and silver became low, and with our country increasing import tariffs to protect domestic goods, the import of foreign goods has become disadvantageous. Japanese textile merchants are therefore investing heavily in establishing and expanding textile factories in Shanghai to avoid high taxes, take advantage of opportunities, and compete with Chinese and foreign counterparts. Currently, the four largest Japanese firms are all adding buildings, increasing the number of spindles and automatic looms to produce finer fabrics, aiming to gain an advantage in the market. Previously, among Japanese factories, only Donghua used automatic looms; now, Nei Wai Cotton Mill No. 9 is adding a total of 1,000 automatic looms, and Shanghai Textile Company's five factories are adding a total of 750. In addition, Yufeng added 30,000 spindles last winter and is now adding another 30,000. Taikang is also adding 20,000 spindles, and both factories have plans to add weaving mills and purchase automatic looms. With the looms of Shanghai Textile and Nei Wai Cotton Mill both scheduled to be installed within six weeks, once production begins, while foreign merchants selling high-quality cotton textiles may not be greatly affected, those selling lower-quality textiles will face a stronger competitor, and China's cotton textile industry, still in its infancy, will inevitably experience even greater pressure.

Report from Weishi County on Suffering from the Calamities of War

The Chinese Red Cross Society received a telegram from Zhang Fang, Chairman of the Henan Relief Commission, stating: "To the esteemed Chinese Red Cross Society, I have received a report from Yang Xuyi, Magistrate of Weishi County, stating that Weishi County has many ravines and the people are poor. The harvest of the two wheat crops was poor, and they were already suffering from hunger and distress when a large number of rebel troops came north and stationed in the cities and villages. They levied funds, vehicles, firewood, and grass, and extorted from wealthy households by exchanging worthless currency, demanding salt money, and levying tobacco taxes, intensifying their oppression. The most difficult and concerning matter is the conscription of soldiers, with each village required to provide over a hundred men, each man requiring a hiring fee of over a hundred yuan. Any delay in meeting the deadline resulted in severe beatings. The total burden over several months amounted to no less than seven million yuan. During the major battle, the artillery fire was deafening, and the cries of anguish shook the fields, a scene too terrible to bear. The back-and-forth trampling ruined homes and shelters. Now, with the arrival of winter, they are exposed to the wind and sleep in the open. I earnestly request assistance and relief. After reviewing the report, the facts are confirmed. Please provide assistance quickly. Zhang Fang, Relief Commission, respectfully requests."

The Nisshin Kinzan Maru Runs Aground and Sinks off Shantou

▲ The Hull is Completely Damaged and Impossible to Salvage

▲ Crew and Comprador Expected to Arrive Tomorrow

The Nisshin Company's Kinzan Maru, carrying mixed grains to Nanhua, ran aground off Shantou. The ship is stuck on the reef and cannot be salvaged. The loss, including cargo, is at least 200,000 yuan. The circumstances of this incident, as investigated and reported by reporters from various sources, are as follows:

▲ Circumstances of the grounding: The Kinzan Maru, fully loaded with soybeans, was en route to Shantou, Xiamen, and Guangzhou to unload its cargo. At 9:40 PM on the 2nd of this month, the ship was about 90 nautical miles off the coast of Shantou. At that time, fog had descended. The captain of the Kinzan Maru intended to arrive in Shantou that night so that the cargo could be unloaded on the 3rd, avoiding any delay in the schedule. Furthermore, this route was familiar to them, and they anticipated no accidents. Therefore, they proceeded in the fog. Unexpectedly, the direction of the channel was obscured by the fog, and the ship ran aground on a submerged reef at 9:45 PM. The bottom of the ship became lodged on the rocks.

▲ Flooding of each hold: The front hold of the Kinzan Maru was breached by the reef, and seawater rushed in. Within moments, the water in the cargo hold reached three feet. Ten minutes later, the second hold also began to flood. It was then discovered that seawater was also entering the engine room. All the lights on the ship went out, and the crew and sailors were terrified, preparing life jackets and rafts to escape. Fortunately, the bottom of the ship was held by the reef, preventing it from immediately sinking, but the water had already reached the main deck.

▲ Naval Rescue: After the accident, the captain urgently sent an SOS wireless signal and set off flares to request assistance. The first to receive the signal was the Japanese destroyer "Take" from Fuzhou, which immediately set sail in the fog to rescue the Kinzan Maru off the coast of Shantou. Upon arriving at the scene, the destroyer did not dare to approach too closely and communicated via wireless radio. At the same time, the "Take" relayed a message to the Nisshin branch in Shantou, ordering them to quickly transport food and other supplies to assist. The "Take" then assumed responsibility for protecting the area to prevent piracy. The Nisshin Shantou branch, upon receiving the report, urgently arranged for the Shanghai-Guangdong liner Songshan Maru, which was returning to Shanghai from Shantou, to load a large quantity of food, fresh water, and rescue supplies and set sail for the scene of the accident. The Songshan Maru launched small motorboats and sampans to deliver the supplies to the Kinzan Maru for the crew and sailors to eat.

▲ Crew Rescue: Since there was no hope of salvaging the Kinzan Maru at that time, the crew prepared to abandon ship. After discussion, the Kinzan and Songshan Maru jointly telegraphed the Shanghai office for instructions. As a result, the company granted approval for the Songshan Maru to rescue the crew, including the comprador Chen Changhua and the accounting staff, and transport them back to Shanghai. Yesterday, the Shanghai office received another telegram stating that the Songshan Maru had left Shantou with the rescued comprador and crew and was expected to arrive in Shanghai tomorrow.

▲ Cargo to be Abandoned: Currently, the Kinzan Maru is grounded on the reef. Although it has not completely sunk, the hole in the bottom of the ship is widening, and the middle hold is also damaged. All the cargo holds are flooded with seawater. The ship has a carrying capacity of 1,710 tons and is loaded with over 10,000 bags of soybeans, which will likely be completely abandoned. However, the company still hopes to salvage some of the cargo on the deck. Therefore, in addition to the captain, a dozen sailors have been left on board to guard the ship and wait for the arrival of tugboats and barges to attempt to unload the cargo on the deck. The Japanese destroyer "Take" is temporarily providing food and protection to the remaining crew.

▲ Repelling Pirates: Pirates are rampant in the waters off Shantou. After the Kinzan Maru ran aground, a group of pirates attempted to rob the ship but were repelled by the Japanese destroyer. The Kinzan Maru was originally a ship of the Osaka Company and was purchased by Nisshin last year for use in expanding its North and South Pacific round-trip liner service. The accident, including the ship, cargo, and crew's luggage, is expected to result in a loss of 260,000 to 270,000 yuan. Fortunately, the ship was not carrying passengers, so there was no loss of life.

Ship Accidents in Heavy Fog

▲ British and Greek Ships Collide

▲ Japanese Ship Runs Aground

▲ Two Ships Damaged: The heavy fog outside Wusongkou lasted for two days. It was not until 3 PM on the afternoon of the fourth that ships began to enter the port one after another. Yesterday, outside Wusongkou at Sanjiashuikou, the Blue Funnel Line's SS Euryades set sail for Shanghai as the fog cleared. As it was sailing, the Norwegian ship Lysefjord, which was carrying water from Shanghai to Wusong to supply a certain ship, approached. At that time, the fog had not completely cleared, and the sea was not very clear. When the two ships drew near, they were unable to avoid each other and collided. The British ship and the Norwegian ship each suffered damage to their hulls, with the damage on both sides being very significant. They entered the port around 5 PM and have reported the incident to the Harbor Bureau for inspection. They will then enter the dock for repairs and discuss the issue of responsibility.

▲ Rokkaku Maru Runs Aground: The Nippon Yusen Kaisha's Rokkaku Maru, sailing from Yokohama to Shanghai, was carrying over 1,000 tons of cargo and about 20 Chinese passengers. On the morning of the fourth, when the ship was about three nautical miles outside the port of Moji, it encountered heavy fog. At that time, the sea lanes were obscured and unrecognizable. The Rokkaku Maru mistakenly sailed onto a submerged reef, and the ship became stuck. The passengers were terrified. Fortunately, the hull was not pierced. The captain immediately telegraphed the head office for help. After eight hours, the NYK dispatched the large steamer Shire to Moji to pull the Rokkaku Maru off the reef and tow it back to the Moji port wharf. Divers inspected the ship and found that the bottom of the hull had been scratched by the reef during the rescue and was unable to sail. It was then decided that the cargo on the Rokkaku Maru would be transferred to the Mikasa Maru, and the passengers would disembark in Moji and transfer to the Mikasa Maru to Shanghai. The Rokkaku Maru was scheduled to enter the port today, but due to the grounding and repairs, it is unable to sail to Shanghai. The Mikasa Maru, which is carrying the cargo and passengers, is not expected to enter the port until the ninth. The company has already notified all passengers.

Two Letters Regarding the RiYa Bank

Accountant Xu Yongzuo sent two letters to accountants Wu Zheng and Pan Zhaobang yesterday, which are recorded as follows:

▲ Shareholder List: "To the esteemed sirs, I have received your letter stating that Yuan Ludeng claims that the company's stock certificate templates and shareholder list were taken by Accountant Xu Yongzuo, and requesting that they be immediately returned for review and reporting. I hereby reply that while I briefly saw these stock certificate templates and shareholder list when I was present at the Rehabilitation Committee, I did not keep them in my possession. I am replying to your letter accordingly. I hope you will investigate. Sincerely, Xu Yongzuo, Accountant. To Wu Zheng and Pan Zhaobang, Accountants."

▲ Registration Issue: "To the esteemed sirs, on the afternoon of the third of this month, I received your letter requesting the transfer of the Shanghai RiYa Bank and Great World Deposit and Tour Department creditor registration documents handled by me. I replied that 'these documents are not the property of the bank or the department and were not within the scope of the receivership entrusted to your accountants on the 27th of last month. Therefore, when I relinquished my liquidation duties, I transferred these documents to the original trustee, the Rehabilitation Committee.' Today (the fifth), I read your advertisement in the newspaper stating that 'creditors who previously registered with Accountant Xu are now requested to come and register with their certificates because Accountant Xu has not transferred the documents, making it impossible to review them.' The advertisement was submitted yesterday, only one day after your letter requesting the transfer of documents. Moreover, registering creditors is not a particularly urgent or pressing procedure. It seems appropriate to wait for the Rehabilitation Committee to transfer the documents. After reviewing the records, I handled registrations for approximately 8,000 households, accounting for two-thirds of all creditors. Among them, there are many women, children, and people who have traveled far to Shanghai. Initially, there were thousands of people every day, vying to register and crowding together, a sight that was heartbreaking. To order these 8,000 households to re-register, considering their circumstances, would be unbearable. Because I have previously handled this case and have a friendly relationship with you, I venture to respectfully submit this letter, hoping that you will consider the public good and the suffering of the majority of creditors, temporarily waive the re-registration to show consideration. The 8,000 creditors will be truly grateful. Sincerely, Xu Yongzuo, Accountant. To Wu Zheng and Pan Zhaobang, Accountants."

The Municipal Council Revises the Nanjing Road Parking Regulations

▲ Announced Yesterday

The revised parking regulations for Nanjing Road of the Shanghai Municipal Council were announced yesterday. Between 8 AM and 6 PM, all vehicles parked on Nanjing Road must not exceed 30 minutes. Permitted parking areas are marked with white paint lines on the roadside. Areas painted red are prohibited from parking at any time. Furthermore, parking is prohibited on the north side of Nanjing Road between (1) 8 AM and 9:30 AM and (2) 1:30 PM and 2:30 PM. Parking is prohibited on the south side of Nanjing Road between (1) 11:30 AM and 12:30 PM and (2) 4 PM and 6 PM.

After the Resolution of the Dispute at the New Ba Xian Qiao Market

▲ All Stallholders Have Moved in and Are Doing Business

The Ba Xian Qiao Market in the French Concession was demolished and rebuilt by the French Municipal Council last spring. During the construction, stalls were temporarily set up in front of the Sino-French School on Route Ghisi Minisini. After more than a year, the new market was completed last month. The Municipal Council announced that it would use a bidding method, which was opposed by all the vendors, so they did not move in. Subsequently, the Chinese Taxpayers Association and Chinese Director Du intervened in mediation, and both sides reached a satisfactory resolution. The Municipal Council notified all the stallholders yesterday, setting tomorrow (the 7th) as the date for all of them to move in and do business. It is reported that the vendors are preparing to move and set up their stalls on schedule.

Mr. David H. Gray Speaks at the Rotary Club Yesterday

The local Rotary Club held a grand and enthusiastic luncheon yesterday. During the event, the club president introduced Mr. David H. Gray, a special representative of Rotary International, who delivered a speech. He began by expressing his gratitude, saying that he felt honored to speak at the Rotary Club in China, which was the first to be established and had the most international members. The organization of Rotary Clubs is widespread throughout the world and is showing substantial progress. Notable achievements have been made by those established in Little Luzon, Shanghai, Tianjin, Beiping, Dalian, Liaoning, and Harbin. In Chile, the first Rotary Club was only officially established four years ago, and now there are more than forty. In Yugoslavia, the organization only existed three years ago, and now there are twenty-five established. The United Kingdom has 350 Rotary Clubs, and London alone has 55. In total, there are currently over 3,200 Rotary Clubs with 154,000 members from 70 countries. In Canada, every city with a population of over 2,000 has a Rotary Club, totaling over 110. He also said that if the Rotary Club did not have its own true value, then these 154,000 outstanding individuals from various countries around the world would not be able to join. Major European countries each have established Rotary Clubs, and South America and North America are also making great efforts. Northern China, Japan, Java, and other places are all making significant progress. From this, it can be seen that the world's major cities are all striving to organize and carry out Rotary Club activities. The greatest purpose of the Rotary Club is that its members must be loyal citizens. There is no place in the Rotary Club for those who do not love their country, because the Rotary Club firmly believes that only those who can truly serve their country are qualified to speak of racial and international friendship. This kind of friendship cannot be achieved through conditions or the rhetoric of diplomats. It is necessary for people around the world to embrace friendship and use this as a guide to interact with each other in order to achieve this goal. The Rotary Club, in view of this, stipulates that all members can attend Rotary Club meetings anywhere. For this reason, 150,000 Rotary Club members from 70 countries have the possibility of close connections at any time. We firmly believe that if you love one person, you will love the country of that person. I remember four years ago, I saw over 9,000 Rotary Club members from 30 countries gathered together for five or six days. What were the good results of such a gathering? The organization of the Rotary Club is international in nature, as can be proven by the selection of successive presidents. From 1928 to 1929, the president was a Mexican, a Catholic. The first vice president was a Scotsman, a Christian. The second vice president was from the United States, and the third was from Chile. These people meet several times a year. The Rotary Club is not a secret organization. Members can invite local or foreign guests to attend at any time, and the club is very considerate of members' actions. The Rotary Club has no religious affiliation. All religions are treated equally and welcomed. It is worth mentioning that the Rotary Club is neither a commercial organization nor is it established to promote the personal business interests of its members. In short, the Rotary Club is a society that brings together the upper echelons of various countries around the world to strive to promote mutual understanding and goodwill and international peace.

Support Meeting for the White Russian Demolition Case

The case of the demolition of White Russian houses in Qingyun Lane, Chongming Road, Hongkou, which concerns all residents of the country, has led more than 20 public organizations in Shanghai to jointly form the Shanghai All-Circles Support Association for the Qingyun Lane White Russian Demolition Case. The first meeting of the association was held at 2 PM yesterday at the Shanghai Citizens United Association's 17th District branch on Sichuan Road. All members were present, and Tang Huilian was elected chairman and Du Yan was the recorder. The chairman reported on the proceedings of the criminal part of the case in the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. Subsequently, the following key issues were resolved: (1) Case of departmental handling. Decided that Zhang Xianfang (Citizens' Association), Wu Hui (Cured Meat Workers' Union), Lu Ganhuo (Ink Workers' Union), Liang Yongyi (Cantonese Cuisine Workers' Union), and Du Chunxun (Puzhi School), five representatives, would be standing committee members; Tang Huilian (17th District Citizens' Association) would be the general affairs officer; Gao Jieyuan (17th District Citizens' Association) would be the accountant; Hu Shouqi (Workers' Union), Cai Xiaohe (Jinhua Ham Association), and Chen Guanghai (Cattle and Sheep Association), three representatives, would be the propaganda officers; Zhao Zhenhui (Pharmaceutical Industry Workers' Union), Chen Daosheng (Guangwei Association), and Guo Zhaowu (4th District Citizens' Association), three representatives, would be the social officers; Du Yan (General Merchandise Workers' Union) would be the secretary; and Jiang Xianhe (17th District Citizens' Association) would be the clerk. (2) Plan for countermeasures against the illegal demolition case. Decided that the passive leader Xing Dingcheng had been subjected to legal punishment, and the issue would be discussed after sentencing. For the active leaders, a letter would be sent to the Municipal Council and a warning would be issued to Wuhua not to collude. Both of these items must be fully addressed within three days. Requests would be submitted to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Nanjing, the Shanghai Municipal Government, and the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters to exert efforts. The details of items C and D would be kept secret. (3) Case of association address. Decided that the Zhongshan Fellow Villagers Association on Qiujiang Road would be used as the address, and Tang Huilian, Liang Yongyi, and Gao Jieyuan would be appointed to contact them. (4) Supplement to the full inauguration photo case. Decided to be handled by the Standing Committee. (5) Case of setting a meeting schedule. Decided to waive the setting and entrust the Standing Committee to be responsible for convening meetings at any time. (6) Temporary motion. The meeting did not end until the clock struck six.

The Municipal Health Bureau Opens a Medical and Health Consultation Section

To facilitate citizens' consultations on medical and health matters, the Municipal Health Bureau has established a medical and health consultation section attached to the First Department. Any citizen who has doubts about medical and health matters and is unable to determine a self-defense plan can submit a written request to the Health Bureau for guidance. The length of the response time will be determined based on the complexity of the consultation. The scope of the response will be a general answer within the possible scope of the matters described in the written request of the consultant. The implementation of matters such as disease diagnosis and medication should still be guided by a physician. For the sake of caution, written consultations are not available for cases where the consultant may have made inaccurate assessments or provided incorrect descriptions.

The Two Bureaus Ban Floating Graves

▲ Deadline for Relocation of Burial by the End of March

▲ Those Exceeding the Deadline Will be Buried on the Spot

▲ Proclamation: The Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau and Public Security Bureau proclaim, for the purpose of proclamation: "After investigation, the floating graves in the city are densely packed, and most of the coffins are thin and have been exposed for a long time, which is a major impediment to public health. Our bureaus have repeatedly proclaimed that coffin owners must relocate the burial themselves. Although all the floating graves in the north and south have been cleared, many others in the countryside are still watching and delaying, and have not complied. Now, out of consideration for the people from other provinces, the deadline is set for the end of March this year. All coffin owners must relocate the floating graves themselves. If the deadline is exceeded, charitable organizations will bury them on the spot. This proclamation is hereby issued for general knowledge. All floating grave coffin owners must comply and not make a mistake. Be sure to."

▲ Announcement: The two bureaus announce that after investigation, floating graves in the city have been repeatedly ordered to be relocated by coffin owners themselves. However, many in the countryside are still watching and delaying, and have not complied. Now, out of consideration for the people from other provinces, the deadline is set for the end of March this year. All coffin owners must relocate the floating graves clearly. If the deadline is exceeded, charitable organizations will bury all floating graves on the spot at their original locations. In addition to the city's announcement for general knowledge, this announcement is specifically issued.

Tenants of Shoufu Lane on Vegetable Market Road Oppose Rent Increases

The houses in Shoufu Lane on Vegetable Market Road in the French Concession, totaling more than a hundred buildings, were previously leased by the Italian Bank. In January of this year, the bank transferred the leasing business to Yong'an Real Estate Company. The company immediately notified all tenants that they must sign new lease contracts with the company within ten days of receiving the letter and increase the rent by 70% of the original amount. Otherwise, they would be required to vacate the premises within the specified period. All the tenants were panicked and gathered on the evening of the previous day at Dongyu Elementary School in the lane to hold a meeting to discuss countermeasures. All the tenants unanimously elected Yang Zhengyong as chairman, who reported on the landlord's letter requiring them to sign new leases and increase the rent by a certain percentage. Next, the 19 articles of the lease contract were read out. All the tenants were very angry and felt that the contents of the contract, such as the pre-payment of a deposit (i.e., small rent) and other various clauses, were extremely harsh. If they agreed, the tenants would have no place to live in peace. They unanimously expressed their opposition. The following methods were then resolved: (1) To organize a tenants' union as a collective countermeasure. (2) Yang Zhengyong, Chen Bangru, Sun Jianqing, Zhang Jieqing, Sun Youliang, Chen Keming, Chen Longfang, Zhu Runqing, Zhu Shifang, Wang Kunshan, and Ling Rongrong were unanimously elected as representatives to be responsible for handling all negotiations. (3) Yang Zhengyong was mutually elected as the chief representative. (4) All unanimously refused to sign the lease contract. (5) First, the tenants' union would send a letter to the landlord stating that the contract was very harsh and difficult to accept, and requesting its automatic withdrawal. (6) All rejected the rent increase. (7) In the event that the landlords forced them to sign the contract and implement the rent increase, they would unanimously refuse and deposit all the rent in the bank as a basis for negotiation. (8) The contents of the landlord's coercive contract and the situation of the huge rent increase would be submitted to the Municipal Government, the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Social Affairs Bureau, the Rent Review Committee, and the Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the French Concession to uphold justice and provide assistance. (9) If necessary, lawyers would be hired to protect them according to the law. (10) All expenses would be shared jointly by all. After unanimous approval, the meeting adjourned.

Local News II

Da Gu Road Foreign Customs Lane: Bandits Continuously Rob Five Families

Police Station Receives Report, Sends Large Force to Arrest

Both Sides Confront, Bullets Fly

One Bandit Killed, Three Bandits Wounded

More Than Ten Additional People Arrested Subsequently

▲ A Chinese Officer Wounded, No Major Injury

At number 1175 Chengqi Lane, Dagu Road, around 9 PM last night, approximately eight or nine bandits entered and robbed multiple homes. Starting from the eastern厢房 (wing room) upstairs and going to the亭子间 (attic room), they robbed a total of five families. The total losses are estimated to be quite significant. The bandits carried away the stolen goods and attempted to escape, but before they left the lane, the local Lao Zha police station received the report and dispatched Chinese and foreign armed detectives to patrol the area. The bandits fled into neighboring houses and opened fire to resist arrest. The police officers returned fire immediately. For a time, the sound of gunfire was constant, like a string of pearls. One bandit was killed on the spot, and three were wounded and captured.

▲ Entire Building Searched, No One Spared West Tibet Road, Dagu Road, Foreign Customs Lane, Chengqi Lane, number 1175. The ground floor is the Zhou Yuanxing tailor shop. Last night at 8:50 PM, seven bandits suddenly staged a robbery. Two bandits stood guard at the front door. After the remaining bandits entered the shop, they brandished handguns, showing them to the workers in the shop to intimidate them into silence. Then, they swarmed upstairs. The tailor shop upstairs had five or six households living there, residing in the main room, eastern and western wing rooms, and the attic, etc. After the bandits went upstairs, four bandits first entered the Zhang family’s eastern wing room. They used searching for stolen goods as an excuse to barge into the room. They then showed their handguns, ordering them not to shout. They opened the boxes and drawers in the room, taking away fox fur coats and ornaments, worth over a thousand yuan. While the four bandits were robbing the eastern wing room, the remaining bandits also worked simultaneously, going to the Ni family in the front building and the Zhang family in the western wing room to rob them. Afterward, the bandits went to the attic room and the back building, opening boxes and overturning baskets, searching everywhere. Countless clothes and jewelry were stolen.

▲ Escaping into Neighboring Houses, Opening Fire to Resist Arrest After the bandits finished robbing, they carried the stolen goods and prepared to go downstairs as a group. Before leaving, they ordered the victims to open the door to see them off, in order to dispel suspicion. The last bandit to leave even took the lock of the main door to prevent the people inside from chasing after them. However, the victims, seeing the bandits leaving, immediately blew whistles at the top of the stairs. The neighbors, hearing the news, also reported to the police station by telephone. Meanwhile, one of the victims ran from the back door to the street and informed the police officer on duty. The bandits, hearing the sound of whistles and shouts, panicked and hurriedly fled into number 1176, a 石庫門 (Shikumen) house to the right of number 1175. The main room of this house also served as a tailor shop, named Zhu Changfa. The shop had many employees who were working. They saw a group of people with anxious expressions suddenly enter through the main door, carrying clothing bundles, and heading straight for the kitchen. They were about to inquire when gunfire erupted. The large police force had already arrived after hearing the news, and the bandits knew things were bad and opened fire to resist arrest. Gunfire Constant, One Dead, Three Wounded After the Lao Zha police station received the news of a large group of bandits staging a robbery, they immediately dispatched armed detectives to patrol the area. The bandits who had fled into number 1176 were now turning back and fleeing for their lives. Except for a few bandits who escaped through the back door, the remaining four bandits were unable to escape and had to open fire in a desperate battle. At the time, the sound of gunfire was constant. Those who didn't know the situation would have thought it was a celebration at the end of the lunar year to thank the gods. Because the bandits were outnumbered, they were shot and fell to the ground. One bandit died on the spot in the lane due to severe injuries. The other three were shot in vital areas and lost their ability to fight. They were all arrested. The wounded were sent to the Public Works Bureau Hospital for treatment and interrogation. The bandit who was shot and killed was not very tall. He was lying at the bottom of the lane against the wall. There were several large patches of blood, shockingly red. Looking up at the wall, there were the words "Wang Deyan's Civil and Military Magic." One could not help but feel saddened for a long time.

▲ Police Station Makes Efforts to Arrest Accomplices The detectives from the Lao Zha police station took the three bandits arrested on the spot back for treatment and interrogation. They revealed the whereabouts of their accomplices, and the police immediately went out to arrest them. By midnight, more than ten people had been arrested. Therefore, it will not be difficult to arrest the remaining bandits one by one in a short period of time. All the stolen goods left behind by the bandits during their escape were also taken back to the police station for the victims to identify. After learning about this robbery case, the reporter went to the scene to investigate and saw that the boxes and belongings in the robbed households were scattered all over the floor after being searched by the bandits, as if they had been through a war. The walls of the Zhu Changfa tailor shop at number 1175 were covered with bullet holes, and the glass of the main door was also broken. When asked about the situation at the time, they only said that the sound of gunfire was like firecrackers going off. The bandit who was killed was lying at the bottom of the lane against the wall. There were several large patches of blood, shockingly red. Looking up at the wall, there were the words "Wang Deyan's Civil and Military Magic." One could not help but feel saddened for a long time.

Two Women Commit Suicide by Poison in the Huizhong Hotel

▲ Arrived Hand in Hand, Chatting and Laughing Freely

▲ Still Not Up by Noon the Next Day

▲ Hotel Attendant Investigates, Discovers Poisoning

▲ The Two Seemed Like Schoolteachers

At the Huizhong Hotel on Hankou Road, two women were found to have committed suicide by poisoning yesterday morning. The circumstances are quite bizarre, and the truth is still shrouded in mystery. The details are as follows: At 12:15 AM the day before yesterday, two fashionable women arrived hand in hand, claiming that their last name was Li and that they were sisters who had just come from Nanjing. The hotel receptionist did not suspect anything and immediately led them to a room on the second floor. The two women were calm and relaxed, chatting and laughing freely. They asked the hotel receptionist if they could get a discount for staying for a few more days. The Huizhong Hotel staff informed them that there were no discounts. The woman surnamed Li paid five yuan in advance and ordered two bowls of noodles from the room attendant. After eating, they closed the door and spoke for a while before falling silent. The room attendant and others assumed that the two women had gone to bed and fallen asleep, unaware that anything was wrong. Until 11 AM yesterday morning, the room attendant, following hotel rules, reminded them that staying past noon would require paying for another day. Since it was almost noon and the two women still hadn't made a move, they opened the door to inquire whether they would continue to stay. They saw the two women fully clothed, with their feet resting on chairs outside the bed, lying side by side as if they were eating opium in a燕子窠 (Yanzi Ke, opium den). The room attendant was shocked. Looking closely, they saw that their faces were pale and they were barely breathing. They knew that they had been poisoned and immediately notified the front desk, who reported to the Lao Zha police station. The police station dispatched police officers to the scene, who took the two women to the hospital for treatment. Later, the room attendant searched the room and found three empty cigarette boxes. The two women had southern accents, had cut their hair, and wore pink wool coats with fur collars. They were about twenty-seven or twenty-eight years old and were quite attractive. They seemed like teachers, it was said.

Dog Racing in the Public Concession to be Prohibited as Scheduled

The Public Concession's ban on dog racing, after the Ming Shen and Liang Yuan respectively responded to the Public Works Bureau's letters on the 14th and 19th of last month, protesting the limited date, the Director-General of the Bureau, Feixin Dun, sent separate letters to the general managers of the two gardens yesterday, informing them that the Public Works Bureau had decided to implement the previous resolution. After March 31st of this year, dog racing will no longer be allowed in the Public Concession. It is expected that the two gardens will comply with the order and stop the races. It is anticipated that from April onwards, the vulgar custom of dog racing will disappear from the Public Concession.

Young Woman Sues Father-in-Law

▲ Father-in-Law Loves Illegitimate Son, Drives Away Her Husband

▲ No Means of Sustenance, Reduced to Beggary

▲ Asks for Inheritance for Her Daughter

▲ Debate Concludes, Awaiting Judgment

▲ Sues Father-in-Law and Husband for Abandonment Local young woman Xu Ding, recently hired lawyer Fan Ming to sue her father-in-law Xu Zhilan and her husband Xu Xiaofu in the local court for conspiracy to abandon her, demanding alimony of 10,000 yuan and 8,000 yuan for the education of her daughter Fengzhen, and requesting provisional execution. The court held a hearing, but it did not conclude because the first defendant, Xu Zhilan, was not present.

▲ Family Fortune of Hundreds of Thousands Ms. Xu Ding now submits additional reasons, stating that her father-in-law Xu Zhilan, listening to false rumors, secretly hid all his property, drove away his legitimate son, abandoned his daughter-in-law, and incited his son to divorce her. His intention is to cut off the lineage of his second son, so that his hundreds of thousands of dollars of wealth will all go to his two illegitimate sons. The legitimate sons, a total of three, have all been driven out to live separately, while the two illegitimate sons live at home. One is destitute and reduced to beggary, while the other spends money like water and lives in luxury. The disparity in treatment is evident.

▲ Mother's Family is Lonely and Destitute Ms. Xu's husband Xiaofu has become disabled from illness. Her father-in-law used to give him 100 yuan per month for living expenses, but has stopped paying in recent years. Her negotiations have been ineffective. As a woman, she is unable to do anything, and it is unknown how she will maintain her livelihood. Furthermore, her mother's family lost her father early and has no brothers. Her mother is over sixty years old and is also lonely and destitute. Her father-in-law's absence from court is intended to delay the case. Her father-in-law has recently been trying to hide his property, which has come to her attention. If she does not take measures to stop him, it will be difficult to enforce the judgment in the future. She specially requests provisional execution to avoid delay.

▲ Withdraws Lawsuit Against Husband The costs of her daughter Fengzhen's marriage and education are requested to be paid in the amount of 8,000 yuan. Her husband Xu Xiaofu was previously listed as the second defendant because her father-in-law bribed him with 200 yuan to come to court and fabricate facts and make false statements. She had no choice but to do so. He realized his conscience in court last time and did not oppose her request. She also does not want to involve him, so she specially requests the court to allow the withdrawal of the part concerning the second defendant Xu Xiaofu to avoid burdening him.

▲ Women Have Property Rights Her father-in-law currently has more than 400,000 yuan in property (residential houses and city houses, totaling more than forty buildings, with monthly rent of more than 2,000 yuan), and a detailed list has been submitted for your review. The deposits in various banks and shares in various companies are kept secret and cannot be investigated. Current laws stipulate that women have the right to inherit property. Her daughter was born to his son and should naturally have the right to inherit the father's share. Now that her father-in-law has driven out his son, as reported in the newspapers, his bias is obvious. If she does not request alimony in advance, the danger in the future is cause for concern, etc.

▲ Xu Zhilan is in Hong Kong Yesterday morning, Judge Zhang Jinjian continued the hearing. The defendant Xu Zhilan was still not present, but he was represented by lawyer Zhong, who stated that the defendant was in Hong Kong. On the second of this month, the defendant's family received a letter sent from Hong Kong on the 26th of last month, and the original letter was submitted as evidence. The judge read the letter and said, "The letter states that your lawyer is fully authorized to act on his behalf." Lawyer Zhong said, "This lawyer is not very clear on what can be admitted and what cannot be admitted."

▲ Defendant's Lawyer's Statement The judge ordered lawyer Zhong to state the defendant's age and origin. Zhong replied that the defendant Xu Zhilan is fifty-nine years old, from Ningbo, and currently lives in Mianjin Lane inside Dadongmen, Shanghai. He used to be in the pharmaceutical business. As for the plaintiff's claim that the legitimate sons were driven out, it is not true. The defendant's eldest son is currently running the Fengchang Newspaper Agency in Xiaodongmen. Xiaofu used to be the manager of a medicinal materials store, but tens of thousands of capital were lost, so the defendant gave him 1,000 yuan in the eleventh year of the Republic to break off their father-son relationship, and another 200 yuan in the nineteenth year to publish a notice, etc. The newspaper was also submitted as evidence. He also stated that the houses in Sanqing Lane where the plaintiff lives belong to the Deji Company. The defendant withdrew his shares last May. If the plaintiff moves back to the defendant's house to live together, the defendant will not refuse. The judge asked whether Xu Xiaofu was the defendant's biological son and whether the plaintiff was his daughter-in-law. Zhong replied that both were correct.

▲ Xu Xiaofu's Plight The court ordered Xu Xiaofu to appear in court (Xu was wearing very ragged clothes and looked like a beggar. His left hand and left foot were paralyzed, so he held a cane and limped into the court, looking quite miserable). The judge asked, "Is your father at home?" He replied, "I don't know." "Where did he go?" The judge asked, "Who wrote the separation agreement?" He replied, "My brother wrote it." The judge asked, "Do you agree to the separation from your father?" He replied, "I don't want to. Although the agreement says 200 yuan, I only received 100 yuan. I have nowhere to go now, please arrange for me, judge." The judge asked, "Why don't you live with your father?" He replied, "My stepmother won't allow it." The judge then ordered the debate to begin. First, the plaintiff's lawyer Fan stated that the plaintiff was young and her husband was disabled. The defendant's actions were too cruel and a judgment should be made. The defendant's lawyer Zhong rose to respond. The judge, understanding the situation, ordered the debate to conclude and set the date for the announcement of the judgment at 3 PM on the 12th of this month.

Regulations on Fingerprinting Criminals

Since the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau started fingerprinting criminal offenders, it has been quite effective. However, the lack of restrictions is not a careful way to protect human rights. The following articles are now formulated for those who should be fingerprinted, and submitted to the Municipal Government for approval. It was issued to all district offices yesterday to be followed. The articles are recorded as follows:

(1) Crimes of sedition and cases of communist reaction are included; (2) Crimes of treason, collusion with the enemy and conspiracy with foreign governments or their envoys to start a war against the people; (3) Crimes of harming foreign relations, offenses against the heads of friendly countries or foreign representatives, and insults to foreign national flags and emblems; (4) Crimes of dereliction of duty, such as embezzlement and bribery by public officials; (5) Crimes of obstructing official duties, such as insulting public officials or using violence and coercion against them in the performance of their duties; (6) Crimes of obstructing elections; (7) Crimes of disrupting order, such as openly gathering crowds with the intention of using violence and coercion, failing to disperse after being ordered to disperse three times, and privately recruiting soldiers; (8) Crimes of escape, escape by prisoners or facilitating their escape; (9) Crimes of harboring criminals and destroying evidence, harboring criminals or forging, altering, and destroying evidence of other people's criminal cases; (10) Crimes of perjury and false accusation; (11) Crimes of public danger, arson, flooding, and explosion of gunpowder, electricity, etc.; (12) Crimes of counterfeiting currency, all counterfeiting of currency and use of counterfeit foreign currency, counterfeit banknotes, and counterfeit coins; (13) Crimes of counterfeiting weights and measures; (14) Crimes of forging documents and seals; (15) Crimes of harming public morals, rape and seduction; (16) Crimes of harming marriage and family, bigamy and abduction; (17) Crimes of infringing on tombs and corpses; (18) Crimes of harming agriculture, industry, and commerce; (19) Crimes of opium, eating and selling prohibited items such as opium, red pills, and morphine; (20) Crimes of gambling, all kinds of gambling and flower clubs; (21) Crimes of murder; (22) Crimes of injury, group fights, mutual fights, and bodily injury caused by car drivers; (23) Crimes of abortion; (24) Crimes of abandonment; (25) Crimes of obstructing freedom, such as illegal confinement and intrusion into other people's homes; (26) Crimes of harming reputation and credit; (27) Crimes of violating privacy; (28) Crimes of theft, stealing other people's property, whether petty theft or pickpocketing; (29) Crimes of robbery, robbery, and kidnapping; (30) Crimes of embezzlement; (31) Crimes of fraud and breach of trust, fraudulent acquisition of property; (32) Crimes of intimidation, extortion by various means; (33) Crimes of receiving stolen goods, buying and storing stolen goods; (34) Crimes of destruction and damage, cases involving violations of prohibitions that are more serious and require fingerprinting of criminal offenders: carrying weapons without the permission of public officials, spreading rumors, vagrant rascals with improper behavior, soliciting prostitution as a clandestine prostitute or facilitating or harboring them, selling aphrodisiacs or abortifacients, assaulting others, using hypnosis for improper purposes, and various cases of tax evasion, such as trafficking in smuggled salt and smuggled alcohol, should also be fingerprinted.

Zou Aizhen's Counterclaim Against Tang Huixuan is Also Unsuccessful

However, during the lawsuit, Zou Aizhen also countersued Tang Huixuan for false accusation and bigamy. The Procuratorate summoned Zou Aizhen to the court alone at 2 PM yesterday afternoon. Suspect in the Assassination of a Foreman

▲ Deceased's Wife Says He Didn't Do It

Zhang Genhan (Ma Pi Lao Si), a foreman of the Japanese-owned Minghua Sugar Factory in Yangshupu, was suspected of being involved in the murder of Gu A'quan, a native of Wuxi, on Pingliang Road. He was detained by the police and sent to the Special District Court for interrogation. Yesterday morning, the police also summoned Gu Chen, the wife of the deceased, and brought Zhang to the court. Judge Xiao interrogated him. According to Gu Chen, her husband was stabbed to death by a knife by a runaway "little fatty". The defendant was also at the scene, but did not do anything. When questioned, the defendant completely denied the charges and hired lawyer Jiang Yiping to defend him. The court ordered the defendant to be returned to custody for sentencing at a later date.

Lawsuit Involving Breach of Contract for Apartment Construction

▲ Chen Weida Sues Wang Shouquan

Chen Weida hired a lawyer yesterday to file a lawsuit in the French Concession court, stating that the defendant Wang Shouquan, acting as the head of the Renji Construction Company, signed a contract with the plaintiff on October 25th of last year to construct a seven-story steel and concrete apartment building on Avenue Joffre for a cost of 71,000 taels. The old materials from the site were sold to the defendant for 6,000 taels. It was stipulated that the project would be completed within nine months. If the house was not delivered after the deadline, a fine of 100 taels per day would be imposed. The defendant's side entrusted Wan Yuanchang Jewelry Store's Wang Zijun as guarantor and provided a receipt as guarantee. However, after the contract was signed, there was no activity for more than three months. There was no wood or carts brought to the construction site. After the plaintiff's investigation, it was discovered that the defendant had used fraudulent means to sell the old materials of the house and then tried to solicit bids for construction with a third party at a tea party. However, no one was willing to contract, resulting in a long delay. It was also discovered that the receipt provided by the defendant was forged. The guarantor Wang Zijun of Wan Yuanchang Jewelry Store had been expelled by his father. All of these actions were false and constituted a violation of Article 363 of the Criminal Code. The plaintiff requested an investigation. The defendant was also represented by a lawyer, who stated that Wang Shouquan was a well-known architect. He had signed a contract with the plaintiff, and the defendant subcontracted the construction to a third party, which was customary in the industry. Later, the plaintiff forced the defendant to issue a cancellation agreement, so the project was stopped. Moreover, since the defendant had sufficient guarantee, how could the plaintiff file a criminal lawsuit? It was illegal and the case should be dismissed. Judge Zhu ordered the guarantor to be summoned to court and the receipt to be transferred to the Land Bureau to verify its authenticity before further investigation.

More Robbers Arrested in Pudong Xiku

Wang Zhang's house in Pudong Xiku was broken into and robbed last year on the eve of the solar New Year. After the incident, the local Third District Police Station learned that the robbers Wang Jialin, Ji Qin Jie, and Yan Fuyu were hiding on Taopeng Road. They sent Chief Zhang with an official letter to the local police station to dispatch more detectives. They secretly went to the area the day before yesterday and arrested the three men. They confessed that Zhang A'bao from Wuxi was also an accomplice. Zhang was then arrested and sent to the Special District Court yesterday. Judge Xiao conducted a preliminary hearing and handed them over to the officers to be taken back for investigation.

Verdict in the Xin Xin Fraud Case

Zhang Shiying, Weng Hengqi, Yang Fuyuan, and others, former employees of the Xin Xin Company, colluded in fraud and embezzled over 180,000 yuan in goods when the company experienced labor unrest in previous years. It was recently discovered and investigated by Detective Wang Changgeng, who detained them and sent them to the Special District Court for interrogation. This was reported previously. Yesterday was the date for the verdict in this case. At 9:30 AM, Judge Zhou took the bench and sentenced Zhang Shiying to one year and six months of imprisonment, and Weng and Yang to one year each. The forged and altered account books were confiscated. The company has recently been carefully planned by Manager Li Minzhou, and its reputation and business have been improving daily.

Woman Commits Suicide by Poison Out of Anger

▲ Conflict with Son from Previous Marriage Du Yuanxiang, a middle-aged man from Shaoxing, lost his wife early and left behind a son named Yongxing, who is sixteen years old this year. After Du's first wife passed away, he married a woman surnamed Gu as his second wife. However, Yongxing was naturally stubborn and easily angered, and Gu was narrow-minded and unable to tolerate him. Therefore, the relationship between mother and son was like that of enemies. The day before yesterday afternoon, they quarreled over a trivial matter, and Yongxing scolded Gu harshly. Gu was very angry and secretly bought opium paste to commit suicide. Someone noticed and took her to Tongren Hospital, but the poison had already taken effect and she could not be saved. She died shortly after. The body was sent to the Forensic Institute on Faelun Road. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Guo Huaipu from the Special District Court arrived at the institute to conduct an examination. He took the bench, and the husband of the deceased, Du Yuanxiang, complained that his son was unreasonable and forced his wife to death, and that his son was now on the run and his whereabouts were unknown. The mother of the deceased complained that her daughter had died at the hands of her nephew and that she would not let it go. Guo then said that although your daughter died, it was due to her own narrow-mindedness. Therefore, she bought opium herself, not that Du Yongxing bought it for your daughter. Therefore, even if you want to punish Du Yongxing, there is no legal basis. He also said that the deceased Du Gu had indeed died by self-poisoning. The body was handed over to her husband Du Yuanxiang for coffin burial.

Japanese Ship Sinks Shanghai-Minhang Boat

▲ Twelve Fall into the River ▲ Wu Laohu Drowns

The boat of He Jinsheng, a boat owner in Minhang Town, travels between Shanghai and Minhang every day. The day before yesterday, He's eldest son Yang Lianyuan loaded cargo and drove the boat to Shanghai. Unexpectedly, when passing the Bailianjing Estuary at noon, the boat was suddenly sunk by a Japanese ship. At that time, twelve people fell into the water. The other boats in the river helped to rescue eleven people, but Wu Laohu, a villager from Lidong Township, drowned because he could not be rescued in time. The patrol boat of the Rescue Bureau recovered the body and notified the family to claim the body for coffin burial. The soybeans and other goods loaded on the boat were all lost. The boat owner He Jinsheng immediately reported the situation to the First District Office of Minhang, and yesterday District Chief Wu forwarded the report to the Shanghai County Government to investigate the Japanese ship involved and negotiate compensation.

Seized Soil-Transporting Car

At about 8 PM the night before last, Captain Niu of the Third Squad of the Zhabei Police patrolled near Datong Road and Zhongxing Road when he suddenly saw a car speeding towards them. He suspected the car and ordered it to stop for inspection. As a result, a large bag of red soil, thirty-one packs of Sichuan soil, and twenty packs of Yun soil were found under the seat. The car driver, Zou Tingyou, and the driver, Zhang Jixin, were taken to the Fourth District Headquarters together with the soil. Zou confessed that a friend asked him to take the goods to Liuhe, but he did not know that it was soil. According to the driver Zhang Weixin, the car belonged to the Huifang Car Company on Avenue Edward. He was rented from our company by Zou, and he did not know that he was transporting soil. The case was submitted to the bureau for investigation.

Inspection of Entertainment Venues

Limiting Seating

The Public Security Bureau and the Public Works Bureau, in order to check the public gathering places in this city such as teahouses, etc., sent personnel to inspect them in 1919, stipulated seating arrangements, so as to avoid dangerous events when the number of people is overcrowded. After this was distributed as a notice, the number of people limited was specified on record. However, recently, it has been reported that although there are many people who follow the regulations, but over time they are ignored.

With the hope of profiting, many people have also privately added seats. It is urgent to strictly rectify and ensure safety. This time, personnel are being sent again to conduct a thorough inspection to see if there have been any changes to the houses recently, and after re-regulating the seats based on the current state of construction, a joint notice will be issued. Starting today, it has been distributed to each jurisdictional district office, ordering them to immediately transfer it to each gathering place and paste it in a prominent place. It is also proclaimed that if anyone violates the regulations and adds seats without permission, they will be arrested and investigated once discovered.

Overview of Business in This City in January of the 20th Year

This month, the Municipal Bureau of Public Works issued licenses for 128 construction projects, 146 repair projects, 136 miscellaneous projects, and 8 demolition projects. Compared to last month, construction, repair, and demolition projects have all decreased, while miscellaneous projects have increased by 50. The total construction area in the city, excluding single-story houses in rural areas, is approximately 28,700 square meters, with an estimated value of approximately 1.32 million yuan, both of which are less than last month. In terms of regional comparison, Fahua ranks first, followed by Hufnan, and then Zhabei. There are six large-scale projects with an estimated value of more than 50,000 yuan, with Zhabei, Hufnan, and Fahua accounting for two each. The details are as follows: (1) A certain Mr. [Surname Omitted] is building residential housing and bathrooms on Quanjia'an Road and Ouyang Road, covering a total area of 1,300 square meters with an estimated value of 44,000 yuan. (2) A Japanese person, Mr. Murayama Yoshimi, is building 22 two-story and three-story residential buildings on Huanglu Road, covering an area of 1,200 square meters with an estimated value of 80,000 yuan. (The above are in the Zhabei District.) (3) Anli & Co. is building two-story commercial housing and residential buildings in Tangjiawan, covering an area of 1,700 square meters, with an estimated value of over 70,000 yuan. (4) A Chinese electrical company is building a cement boiler room covering an area of 750 square meters, with an estimated value of 57,000 yuan. (The above are in the Hufnan District.) (5) The Academia Sinica is building an experimental laboratory on Yuyuan Road, covering an area of 1,600 square meters, with an estimated value of over 211,000 yuan. (6) A certain Mr. [Surname Omitted] is building two one-story residential buildings on Yuyuan Road, covering a total area of 600 square meters, with an estimated value of 72,000 yuan. (The above are in the Fahua District.) This month, new houses are mostly built on open land, so the demolition area only accounts for 2,500 square meters. Due to fewer projects, enforcement matters are also relatively simple, with only 96 cases, mostly due to non-compliant projects, accounting for about two-thirds of the total. This month, routine inspections of public buildings were conducted, including 10 theaters and 212 tea gardens.

Education News

Important News: Representatives of the Jiangxi Education Circle Petition in Beijing

▲ Educational Funds Will Have Proper Arrangements

▲ The Custody Issue is Being Discussed

Representatives of the Jiangxi education community, including Chen Yingchun, Zhu Yuanqing, Deng Tianmin, Tu Gang, and Yan Jiayuan, have arrived in Beijing and have been petitioning various parties for days. A general decision has been made. However, the representatives, noting that the Jiangxi Provincial Government had resolved that the Jiangxi Education Fund be independently managed by the Education Department, but in recent years, due to the impact of banditry, education fees have been in arrears for as many as six or seven months. Now that the central government has recovered the salt surcharge, they are repeatedly requesting the central government to instruct the West Bank Tax Transport Bureau to directly hand over the education funds allocated by the central government to Jiangxi Province to the education authorities for safekeeping. The process of their petition is briefly recorded as follows: (1) First, they went to the Central Party Headquarters. Secretary-General Chen was absent due to important business and delegated the Director-General of the Liaison Section to meet them, who promised to convey the points raised to the Secretary-General and submit them to the Standing Committee for approval and transfer to the National Government for review and handling in accordance with the party's program. (2) Next, they went to the National Government and were met by Chairman Jiang and Secretary Zhu. They then went to the Executive Yuan and were met by Secretary Liu. The representatives immediately stated their petition opinions: 1. Request the central government to subsidize the Jiangxi Education Fund with 2.07 million yuan from foreign tax items. 2. Request the central government to instruct the West Bank Tax Transport Bureau to directly hand over the funds to the education authorities for safekeeping in accordance with the established case. Secretary Liu said that the academy's directive on rectifying the style of study has clearly stated that education funds should not be lacking in the slightest. The Ministry of Education already has a plan for the education fund issue in various provinces, which can be resolved at the state council meeting in three days. (3) They then went to the Ministry of Education, where they were received by Vice Minister Chen. After the representatives stated their opinions, Chen replied that the central government would definitely come up with proper solutions because the education funds in various provinces had been affected by the abolition of levies and the unification of salt taxes. In addition, regarding the arrears in Jiangxi's education fees, he will earnestly consult the Jiangxi Provincial Government to allocate funds. Finally, Deng Tianmin, in the name of the manager of students studying in Japan, stated that the students studying in Japan were in extreme distress due to huge arrears and asked for relief. Chen replied that within the possible scope, he would allow efforts to be made. Next, they went to Finance Minister Song, who was not in Beijing but in Shanghai. The Secretary-General met them and said that the Jiangxi education fee had been ordered to be handled by the Salt Affairs Administration and other issues, such as increasing the 700,000 yuan and independent safekeeping, would have to wait for Minister Song to return to Beijing and ask for instructions. Finally, they went to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and were met by Secretary Luo, who said that the central government had approved that the Jiangxi education fee would still be allocated from the salt surcharge from March. The representatives then reiterated that the Jiangxi education fee budget for this year must be at least 2.7 million yuan and that the independent custody of the education fund was decided by the 71st Provincial Affairs Conference in Jiangxi Province in the 17th year and was also stipulated by National Government Order No. 123. Therefore, they requested that the West Bank Tax Transport Bureau be instructed to directly hand over this fund to the education authorities for safekeeping in accordance with the established case in order to comply with the central government and provincial government laws and regulations. Secretary Luo replied that the custody issue would be reported to the head of the department and asked for instructions from the minister. In short, the ministry is clearly aware of the difficult situation of the education community in the province and has its own solutions. It seems that the province's education fee issue has been properly resolved. Therefore, the representatives will return to Jiangxi to report everything as soon as the reply is received.

The Second Day of the Shandong Educational Administration Meeting

Jinan Correspondence: The first and second meetings of the Shandong Provincial School Education Administration Conference have been reported in the previous letter. Today (the 3rd) at 9:00 AM, the third standing committee meeting was held at the Women's Normal School. 46 people attended, chaired by He Siyuan, and recorded by Yang Peng. The meeting was opened as usual to report matters: (A) The monthly recurring expenses saved by each school may not be used as temporary expenses without approval (reported by the First Section). (B) The budget book for temporary expenses of each school regarding repairs and construction should be attached with an estimated bill and detailed drawings, and the budget book for purchases should be attached with a list of item names, unit prices, and total amounts for verification and transfer (reported by the First Section). (C) The budget book for each month of each school must be written and not printed (reported by the First Section and the Audit Committee). (D) The deadline for the hall to solicit the general situation of Chinese language teaching in various secondary schools has passed, and it should be submitted quickly for verification and printing (E) Within two months after the start of each semester, each school should submit the content of each subject's teaching materials and the progress of teaching to the hall (reported by the Second Section). (F) Within one month after the end of each semester, each school should submit the actual teaching materials and the actual teaching situation to the hall (reported by the Second Section). Matters for discussion: (A) The issue of service for normal school graduates was resolved without restriction. At this point, He Siyuan asked for leave, and Lai Zhizhong took over as chairman. (B) The issue of setting up summer training classes in provincial schools was resolved to be retained and discussed again after the director of the hall explained. (C) The issue of the salary standards for teachers and staff in secondary schools was explained by Pi Songyun, the head of the Third Section. At this point, the meeting adjourned.

Ministry of Education Sends Personnel to Take Over China Public School, Appointing Gu Shusen, Zhu Yingpeng, and Cen Dechang as Members

Nanjing, 5th (Central News Agency): The Ministry of Education previously sent Counselor Zhu Baoqin and Secretary Guo Youshou to Shanghai to investigate the turmoil at China Public School.
