Municipal Education Bureau Prepares for Literacy Campaign

▲ Held on February 21st, 22nd, and 23rd

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau is aware that there are a large number of illiterate people in this city, and a literacy campaign is held every year. It is reported that the bureau has scheduled the third literacy campaign to be held on February 21st, 22nd, and 23rd, and has appointed Li Dachao, Yang Peiwen, Chen Songchun, Chen Duanzhi, Wang Keyong, Zhang Meisun, Yao Gengkui, Zhou Shang, Zhang Fufeng, Shao Minghe, Cao Zhen, Lu Hailan, Xu Baozhong and other thirteen people as members of the literacy campaign committee. The outline of the literacy campaign method formulated by the committee is recorded below: (1) Purpose: 1. Awaken public interest in literacy, 2. Refresh public perception of literacy, 3. Arouse public sympathy and support for the plan to popularize literacy education. (2) Target: 1. Let illiterate people know the importance of literacy, 2. Persuade literate people to fulfill their teaching duties, 3. Persuade wealthy people to help implement the funding, 4. Other people who directly or indirectly contribute to literacy, expanding the ranks of the literacy campaign. (3) Otherwise: 1. To popularize the whole city, 2. To use very little funding to achieve great results, 3. To establish a solid connection with the public education cause sponsored by the bureau. (4) Measures: 1. The number of members of the organizing literacy campaign committee is tentatively set at 13. The director of the bureau will separately appoint or commission people who are enthusiastic about public education in the city and staff members of the bureau. 2. The literacy campaign committee may set up three sections according to business needs: general affairs, publicity, and entertainment. A director will be set up for each section, and several staff members will be set up. The director will be mutually elected from among the members, and the staff members will be selected from among the members and hired. 3. The date of the literacy campaign is scheduled to be held on February 21st, 22nd, and 23rd. 4. Commercial meetings, youth gatherings, and juvenile lecture groups will be held in the Central Auditorium on February 21st, 22nd, and 23rd, and celebrity lectures will be given. The entertainment programs will be handled by the committee by writing letters to the Juvenile Lecture Group, Vernacular New Drama Comrades Association, Youth Association, Music Group, and Li Changjian and Han Langan, etc. The lectures will be handled by the association by writing letters to party and state celebrities. Admission tickets will be printed and distributed to the people before February 16th. 5. Contact major newspapers and small newspapers in the city to allocate a 2-inch to 4-inch space in each issue to publish materials related to the literacy campaign, which will be provided by the committee. 6. Contact major newspapers in the city to compile and print three special issues of the literacy campaign on February 21st, 22nd, and 23rd. 7. Contact major cinemas in the city to add literacy campaign promotional advertisements to each show on February 21st, 22nd, and 23rd, and the materials will be provided by the committee. 8. Send a letter to the Propaganda Department of the Municipal Party Department, ordering the district sub-departments to start publicizing the literacy campaign on February 21st, 22nd, and 23rd. 9. The bureau will order the principals of municipal schools with two or more classrooms in the city to lead all teachers, staff, and senior students on February 21st, 22nd, and 23rd to carry out the literacy campaign near the school. The scope of the materials includes entertainment lectures and posters, etc., which will be provided by the committee. 10. Public schools in various districts that are preparing will officially start classes on March 1st. 11. Order the Municipal Public Education Center to contact local agencies to carry out the literacy campaign on the spot. 12. Order all public schools to convene graduates from previous years to carry out literacy campaigns in nearby areas. 13. Order all sports fields to distribute leaflets and pictorials promoting literacy to everyone who enters the field on February 21st, 22nd, and 23rd, and the materials will be provided by the committee. 14. Regularly convene factory owners or managers of major factories and store owners or managers of major stores in the city to hold a talk, explain the importance of literacy, and ask them to assist in the work of the association. 15. Regularly convene storytellers in the city to hold a talk, explain the importance of literacy, and ask them to publicize it widely when telling stories. 16. Install slogans and pictures promoting literacy in main thoroughfares.

Mayor Zhang's Speech

▲ To Correct Errors in the Record of the Education Bureau's Directive

Yesterday, Mayor Zhang spoke with reporters to address slight errors in the record of his directive at the inauguration ceremony of Director Xu of the Education Bureau the day before. He stated that during the supplementary inauguration ceremony of Director Xu of the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau on the 4th of this month, he quoted the resolution of the Third National Congress on political reports regarding education, saying that there were six abuses in current education, namely: (1) an abundance of schools, (2) an abundance of school operators, (3) an abundance of teachers, (4) an abundance of teaching materials, (5) an abundance of enrollment, and (6) an abundance of admissions to higher education. These six abuses further lead to four evils and form three harms, etc. However, yesterday's newspapers mistakenly recorded the six "abuses" as six "difficulties" in his speech, resulting in inconsistencies in the meaning of the entire text. Fearing that readers may not notice the details, he specifically asked you to correct them.

Civil Middle School Sued

(Educational Press) The Civil Middle School in Dananmen, Shanghai, has been operating for many years. Recently, it was suddenly sued for violating departmental regulations, encroaching on school funds, and other items. It is reported that the director of the Municipal Education Bureau has deemed the case important and has appointed Inspector Li and Section Member Xu of the bureau to thoroughly investigate and handle the matter.

The Shanghai Special City Party Department's Training Department has completed the citywide middle school student party ideology essay competition on the 31st of last month. Students from Jinan, Zhengfeng, Qianye, Guangdong, Renhe Chengzhong, Peiming Hujiang, Junyi, Yucai, Dexin, Wusong, Xiangshi, Jingye, Guangzhao, Wuben and other schools participated. The evaluators have been hired as follows: Yuan Yeyu (reporter of the Republican Daily), Lou Tongsun (member of the Legislative Yuan, director of the Nanjing Training Department), Pan Gongzhan (director of the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau), Tao Baichuan (member of the Municipal Executive Committee), Yang Fayuan (director of the Municipal Propaganda Department), Xu Wentai (former secretary of the Municipal Education Bureau), Tong Xingbai (concurrent chief evaluator, director of the Municipal Training Department). It is said that the results will be fully announced by the 25th of this month at the latest.

Representatives of Students Studying in France Come to Shanghai to Petition

丨To Promote the Problem of Students' Studying丨

▲ Cai Jie Min and Chu Minyi Both Agreed to Help Enthusiastically

▲ To Wait for Li Shizeng to Go South to Jointly Plan Proper Measures

After the end of the European War, Li Shizeng, seeing the domestic industrial recession and the immaturity of science, advocated that young students go to France to study. Between the years 8 and 9 of the Republic of China, as many as 2,000 people went to France. At that time, China and foreign countries were in an uproar, opening a precedent in the study abroad community. Later, France's economy gradually changed, and the Northern Warlord Government at that time was indifferent to this matter, causing the majority of young people to fall into a dangerous situation. After the establishment of the revolutionary government, when Li was sent to France, the remaining students were only a hundred or so. They had been working and studying in France for ten years. Now, they are unable to complete their studies due to economic limitations. Therefore, they appointed Liao Junyi, the secretary of the student union, as a petition representative to request Li to solve the problem of studying. At that time, he tried to find a way on the spot, but he was unable to solve it completely. Liao, bearing the heavy trust of the students, at his own expense, returned to the country from France in the autumn of the year before last, hoping to achieve his goal and then stop. He also stated that he would not accept financial assistance from any party, would not participate in other movements before the petition task was completed, would not apply for subsidies, and would not handle funds. After the matter was completed, he would immediately return to France. Liao has been back in the country for more than a year, running around in Beijing, Shanghai, and Peiping for the students, and has been deeply supported by the political and educational authorities. The funds he has secured include a 50,000 yuan appropriation approved by the Executive Yuan of the Central Government and a 28,000 yuan appropriation approved by the Hebei Provincial Government for recurring expenses. The items that are still to be discussed include a subsidy of 140,000 yuan approved by the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Committee and 30 additional places for work-study students approved by the University of Lyon, France. Last year, Liao went to Hunan to appeal for students from Hunan, but due to the repeated ravages of soldiers and bandits in the province, public and private finances were in difficulty, and there was no result. Yesterday, he came to Shanghai to meet with Cai Jie Min, Chu Minyi, and the relevant authorities, asking them to expedite the realization of the funds that have been secured and the items that need to be discussed before this year's summer break so that the students can enroll on schedule. It is said that Cai, Chu, and others have all agreed to help enthusiastically, and once Li Shizeng arrives in Shanghai, they will jointly plan a practical solution.

White Goose Art Exhibition in Recent Days

The fifth exhibition of student works by the White Goose Painting Institute has attracted thousands of Chinese and foreign visitors since its opening on January 31st. People are amazed at the various works on display. The students' works, such as Hu Zhongping's watercolor sketches, which are fresh and lively, and Luo Tianmin's mature colored oil paintings, and the works of Zhou Shouxian, Shen Songgen, Xia Lianzhen, Wang Jialong, etc., all show genuine research efforts. The works of female researchers such as Gao Huijuan, Liu Tongxia, Pan Ming, Xu Haiou, and Xu Huilan, with their exquisite colors and sketches, are particularly rare. As for the guidance, Chen Qiucao's two large-scale nude oil paintings have a strange composition that evokes a sense of perseverance. Fang Xuegu's portrait of two ladies, PK, has a beautiful color tone, and the landscape works are even better. Pan Sitong's watercolor paintings are bold and the painting style is unique, which can be called the only one in the country. Du Xueou's still life landscape oil paintings are numerous, and the greatness of life can be seen in the quietness, which is a rare masterpiece. It is said that the exhibition date is set to close on the 6th.

Jinnan Football Team and Zhenru Basketball Team's Philippine Expedition (6)

(Report from our reporter Wen Chu from Manila on January 20)

(1) Sino-Western Alumni Banquet

The Sino-Western School Alumni Association of Little Luzon held a banquet for the Jinnan Football Team and Zhenru Basketball Team on the 17th of this month. It was originally scheduled for last night, but it was changed to today because there was a basketball game at 6:30 PM yesterday. The grand occasion is also worth recording.

History of the Alumni Association

The Sino-Western School has a history of more than 30 years and is the oldest overseas Chinese school in the Philippines. The number of students attending classes day and night has exceeded 1,000 for several years. There are now thousands of graduates who are scattered in various fields of commerce, academia, and reporting, as well as in bank services and customs translation (the translators in the immigration department of the current Mariveles Customs are all graduates of the school). Famous lawyers in the overseas Chinese community such as Gao Zuchuan and young philanthropist and sportsman Lin Zhuguang were all top students at the school more than ten years ago. Therefore, in terms of the unity of various overseas Chinese organizations, the alumni association can be called the backbone. Because the members have been playmates since they were young, when they grow up, they will become a kind of combination, which naturally has many unspeakable interests.

Relationship with Jinnan School

In terms of students, those who return to the country to transfer to school and seek higher learning naturally come to this only highest institution of higher learning for overseas Chinese. Therefore, more than half of the current Jinnan Alumni Association in the Philippines are former alumni of Sino-Western School. In terms of faculty members, the former principals of Jin University, Jiang, Ke, Zhao, and the current principal Zheng, and Mr. Liu Shimu all communicate with each other. The leader of this time, Chen Xuege, was also a former teacher at the school and was sent to the United States for further studies with the financial support of Mr. Lin Zhuguang. Therefore, before the teams arrived, when the association was preparing to welcome them, they first welcomed them by radio to the ship, and when they arrived ashore, the combined team went to the pier to welcome them, expressing their utmost sincerity and love.

Banquet Circumstances

Held at the Mignon Hotel, a Western establishment, with the entire hall rented. Outside, in large Chinese and English characters, was written "Sino-Western School Alumni Association Banquet and Southern Football Team, Zhenru Basketball Team." Five or six alumni, including a lawyer named Gao Zuchuan and the Chairman of the Timber Merchants Association, Mr. Xu Youchao, wore lapel pins and greeted guests. Party and national flags, along with the flags of the United States and the Philippines, were hung all over the front windows. The banquet tables were arranged in a shape. At seven o'clock, the guests began to arrive, numbering over a hundred alumni and twenty-nine football and basketball team members. (Mr. Chen Zhenhe did not attend either banquet because the first competition was not a resounding victory.) Among the guests were Mr. Chen Yinglai of the General Chamber of Commerce, Mr. Lin Xijin, Chairman of the Overseas Chinese Education Association, Mr. Xue Minlao, a lawyer, Dr. Zheng Han, principals of various bridge schools, reporters from various Chinese-language newspapers, current and retired teachers from Sino-Western schools, and over eighty prominent figures from the business community, totaling over two hundred attendees. The number of attendees at past alumni association banquets had never been so large, and the punctuality was also unprecedented. (Overseas Chinese banquets are officially set for seven o'clock, but the number of people often doesn't arrive until eight o'clock.) This shows that the overseas Chinese community is paying considerable attention to this returning team. During the banquet, Mr. Lin Zhuguang, the main speaker, outlined the purpose of the meeting, briefly stating that the most inspiring thing for overseas Chinese during these twenty years of the Republic of China

Shanghai Table Tennis Federation Staff Meeting

▲ Hiring Honorary Advisors to Jointly Raise Funds

▲ Women's Team Competition Registration Begins Immediately

▲ Men's and Women's Singles Tournaments to Be Held Separately

The Shanghai Chinese Table Tennis Federation held its first staff meeting the night before last at the Guangdong Table Tennis Team's meeting room. Chairman Wu Jiangleng and Secretary Fei Jikang recorded the following resolutions: (1) Regulations for Competition Work and Responsible Persons: (Resolved) The General Secretary, Xu Duo, is responsible for various competition tasks and team requests for rescheduling. (2) Rotating Duty for Association Affairs and Setting Office Hours: (Resolved) Five staff members will rotate duty for association affairs on Mondays, Wednesdays, and Fridays. If teams have business, they should contact the association office on time. (3) Methods for Expanding the Association's Funds: (Resolved) The Chairman will jointly plan with the General Secretary to hire prestigious advisors to jointly raise funds. (4) Gu's Cup Letter Requesting to Handle the Finals and Sending Ruan Yaohui to Discuss Everything in Person: (Resolved) Upon investigation, the Gu's Cup was not registered with this association, and the current team is not a member. We are now making a special accommodation to handle it. The team should complete the above procedures according to regulations, and this association will handle all finals matters according to the request in the letter. (5) Holding a Women's Team Competition: (Resolved) Registration begins immediately and closes on February 25th. The competition will start on March 1st. Each team can register seven players, with a membership fee of one yuan and no registration fee. (6) Scheduling Men's and Women's Singles Championships to be Held Separately: (Resolved) To begin immediately after the end of the United Cup. (7) Establishing Table Tennis Rules for Unification: (Resolved) To collect the rules compiled by Wu Jiangleng, Yu Binqi, and Wu Maoqing and revise the Shanghai Table Tennis Federation standard rules, which will be distributed to various teams to ensure unification. The editing will be the responsibility of the staff. (8) Scheduling Regular Staff Meetings: (Resolved) To hold a meeting every two weeks during office hours on Mondays, etc. It is heard that the association staff is scheduled to have a photo taken this Sunday at Hollywood.

(2) Honorary Advisor Meeting

The prestigious advisors invited by Jiannan University, after meeting at a dinner party led by team leader Chen Zhang'e, elected Chen Yinglai, Li Ziquan, and Xue Minlao as directors. At 7:00 PM on January 20th, the three directors invited the advisors to a dinner at the Datong Club to discuss methods for assisting Jiannan University. Those present that day included Chen Yinglai, Xue Minlao, Consul General Kuang, Xue Fenshi, Chen Yuanhe, Zheng Hanqi, Cai Shaojing, Yang Kongying, Yu Yongrong, Zhan Houshi, Lin Xijin, Wang Quansheng, Li Fengrui, Chen Zhang'e, Yan Fuchu, and two representatives from the Jiannan Alumni Association. After the meal, Chairman Chen Yinglai asked Mr. Zhang'e to state the purpose of inviting the advisors this time and to mention that the football and basketball teams were scheduled for five matches until the 28th. The Charity Association wanted to invite the teams to play a few more matches to raise more income to return home on February 10th, and he would be responsible for the accommodation fees for these ten days. Mr. Chen declined. During the discussion, it was noted that Jiannan University, as an overseas Chinese institution of higher learning, was trying to develop sports but was limited by funding, and the overseas Chinese business situation was declining and could not provide sufficient donations. It was suggested that if the Charity Association were to hold additional matches, they could consult with the Consul General and the Chairman of the General Chamber of Commerce. These two gentlemen would negotiate the admission fees, with some going to the Charity Association and some going to Jiannan University to develop sports. Then, the Consul General would jointly the Principal agree to the players staying for more games This plan, after being agreed upon by the majority, also discussed setting up a grand farewell party when the athletes were about to leave, with the prestigious advisors as the main body, and elected members to be responsible for the preparations.

Woman丨Thank you. I also think about you often. Can you come to my house tonight to see me?

Young man (looking overjoyed)丨I couldn't be happier! I'll definitely come tonight, no matter what. But do you really need me?

Woman丨Of course. I've been so lonely since my little pug died.

▲ A丨I heard your child swallowed a gold coin the other day. How is he now?

B丨Speaking of that, it really makes me sad.

▲ A丨Surely the gold coin is still in his stomach, hasn't come out yet?

B丨It came out, but somehow, the gold coin has changed color and can't be used anymore.

▲ A丨Then have you ever seen anyone faint without turning pale?

B丨Of course I have. I've seen several.

▲ A丨Who are they?

B丨Black people with naturally black faces.

Record of the Skilled Shooter Zhong Shaokui · Yue · Fu

Zhong Shaokui is from Tingzhou, western Fujian. He previously served as a battalion commander under Zhang Zhen of the Independent Fourth Division and Tan Shuqing of the New First Army. He is currently a military leader of the Tingzhou Hometown Rescue Corps. He possesses extraordinary skills. From a young age, he was proficient in martial arts, and he has particularly deep research into handgun shooting techniques. It is said that when he was twelve years old, bandits surrounded and looted the pawnshop next to his house. He was able to kill two bandits with a shotgun, thus settling the matter. His father was amazed and had him study military affairs. Later, as an officer, he still made shooting practice a daily routine. After five years, his skills greatly improved. Now, within twenty steps, his handgun shots rarely miss.

Last autumn, I returned to my hometown on business and met Shaokui at the Shanghang military station. We were as happy as if we had known each other all our lives. One afternoon, while walking in the western suburbs, we happened to see a wild mouse foraging on the ridge. I said, "You are skilled with guns, why don't you shoot it?" He listened to my words, took out a Browning, and fired a shot. The mouse fell dead on the spot. I praised him incessantly. He said, "This is just like the oil vendor in Ou Yangxiu's story, 'There's nothing to it, just practice makes perfect.'" We then passed a farmhouse where a large spider had built a web on the eaves. He said to me, "Now I will try out my skills. You stop. I can shoot this spider from ten steps away." Soon, there was a loud bang, and the spider was gone. At this time, the farmer's children did not know the details of the person who had come and laughed, saying, "The spider is afraid of the sound of the gun and ran away in a panic." I told them, "The spider is not afraid of the sound of the gun. It was actually killed by the bullet." The children said, "Is that so? If you can ask this gentleman to fire another shot and break the eastern end of this spider web, we will believe it." I asked Shaokui. Shaokui said, "Good. Let's try it." He held the handgun, aimed slightly, and fired. The eastern end of the spider silk broke. The children saw a part of the spider web fluttering in the wind. They all clapped and said, "Amazing! How divine is this gentleman's marksmanship!"

According to the villagers, in the autumn of the year Ji Si, Shaokui planned to capture the bandit leader Tang Xue

in the banquet. The subordinates surrendered their weapons. Last year, in May and August, the Fujian Western Red Bandits, led by Fu Bocui, launched two major invasions of Shanghang City, but were defeated. His wife, Madam Mou, also knows marksmanship and once assisted her husband in suppressing bandits. Details are in the Shantou and Xiamen newspapers. Many people know about it. (Thank you for the reward)

The Bridegroom Returning from the Bandit Den Jing Mengdie

As the year ends, banditry becomes more rampant. In the four regions of Changzhou, kidnappings are frequently heard of. However, some encounters are fortunate and some are unfortunate. In a village near Benniu, there was a son of the Zhang family. He had been newly married for just three days when bandits suddenly arrived, looting the contents of the bridal chamber and taking the groom away, demanding a ransom of a thousand gold pieces. However, the Zhang family was not wealthy. At that time, the bride's beautiful dream had just come true. Suddenly, a fierce wind arrived, and she saw her beloved husband leave the bridal chamber and enter the tiger's den, a separation worse than death. Her pain can be imagined. She rushed to kneel before her father and begged him to find a way to save her husband. The father frowned and said, "The family is poor. Even your wedding expenses were borrowed. I am already in debt. Where would I get the huge sum to satisfy the bandits' desires?" The bride knew that it was impossible to plan anything. She cried all night, sitting and waiting for dawn, truly "tears drenched the handkerchief, dreams unfulfilled." The next morning, she returned home and consulted her parents. However, the bandits' demands were extravagant, and they could not help. They were worried and had no ideas. Later, the bandits discovered the truth about the Zhang family and the bride's suffering. They generously reduced the price to a hundred gold pieces and sent word to the Zhang family. The bride was overjoyed and tried to raise the money to save her husband. The next day, Zhang's son indeed returned. From head to toe, he was brand new. His hat, shoes, and clothes were all gifts from the bandits. The looted items were also returned in full. However, one suitcase was no longer the old one. The bandits had damaged one corner of it, so they bought a new one to replace it. As Zhang's son left, firecrackers were set off, and wedding congratulations were given to send him off. The people on the roadside watched the groom, almost forgetting that he was a survivor of a robbery. This was truly great fortune in misfortune. Bandits also have a code of conduct. Is that true?

Strange Child Huang Yingdai

Yesterday, a guest came from my hometown and mentioned that a certain family had given birth to a child with physiological differences from others. I recorded it immediately.

▲ Concubine Gives Birth to a Son Near Zhujiage, there is Anzhuang Town, with waterways in all directions and numerous rivers, where bandits often appear. In the town, there is a certain family that is moderately wealthy. They are already middle-aged but have no heir, which is a regret. So, they took in a concubine last year, surnamed Jiang. The concubine became pregnant, and the whole family was delighted. On the day of delivery, she gave birth to a son. The family was overjoyed to have a son in their old age.

▲ Strange Physiology However, after the child was born, upon closer inspection, his physiology was different from that of ordinary babies. The genitals were not very different, but another object was revealed at the anus, about five or six fen long, identical to the genitals in front. One person with two penises. Those who heard about it thought it was a monster, and the family was quite unhappy about it. They urgently wanted to find a way to get rid of it, but it was a pity to kill it and pitiful to abandon it. They were in a dilemma.

▲ Sent to the Infant Asylum Afterwards, after repeated discussions with relatives and friends, they decided to send the child to the infant asylum. So, they hired an old woman to take a boat at night and send him to the Zhujiage Infant Asylum. The old woman knew that this child was different and was uneasy, fearing that the infant asylum would discover it on the spot and send him to the authorities. Paris Stories (24)

Fourteen The Roman Colonial Era Open-Air Theater

There are many cities in the world that are specifically for people to search for historical sites, such as those ancient civilizations along the Mediterranean coast. Conversely, in many newly built countries, such as the Americas, their cities are just a display of youth and strength. If we visit Rome, the capital of Italy, we will definitely feel that the past is conquering the present. Everywhere is a recollection of history. Those ruined wells and crumbling walls are filled with thousands of years of secrets. But when we visit New York, our feelings are completely different. We only have amazement at modern civilization. If we happen to think back to yesterday, it only makes us admire today's progress even more. But Paris is completely different. It is neither Rome nor New York, but it can be said to have both Rome and New York. Paris is an ancient yet new capital. Here, the latest material civilization of the twentieth century shines alongside the ancient ruins of two thousand years ago. After walking around those prosperous streets near the National Opera House, you can return to the small alleys in the Latin Quarter to stroll and feel that you have traversed several centuries in a day. After emerging from the newest subway, the epitome of modern civilization, you may see a very old building from hundreds of years ago or a famous sculpture that has experienced many rises and falls on any street you walk down. The past and the present are mixed together and do not make people feel unharmonious. This is the characteristic of Paris.

The best representation of this mixed image of ancient and modern is the Roman colonial era open-air theater in the 5th arrondissement. Not far from the Botanical Garden, near a very modern street called rue Monge, we can see a circular square surrounded by layers upon layers of orderly stone steps, just like the seats of the newest theaters that gradually rise. This is a relic left by the Romans in ancient Paris Lutece during their rule of the Gaulish people fifteen hundred years ago. It is now commonly called Les arenes de lutece, the Lutece Arena

she fled.

▲ Discovery of a Secret The staff in the infant asylum saw that the old woman looked flustered and knew there must be something unusual, but they did not suspect that the child had two penises. Later, when a nurse in the asylum was changing diapers, she saw that the child had another object growing behind his buttocks and realized the secret. She immediately ordered someone to go to the market to look for the old woman, but she was already gone without a trace.

▲ How Many Died Afterwards, the infant asylum could do nothing. They could only temporarily take care of this strange child. Unexpectedly, after this child entered, six or seven other babies in the asylum died one after another. For a time, superstitious people said that this child was an ominous object and urged the person in charge to get rid of him as soon as possible to avoid future troubles.

▲ Corpse Exposed on the Street The person in charge of the asylum believed that the deaths of the other children had nothing to do with this child, so he continued to take care of him as usual. However, not long after, this child also died of illness. The asylum, because the child's physiology was quite strange, exposed his corpse on the streets after his death. For a time, crowds gathered to watch, and they all exclaimed in astonishment.

Wu Men Fun Anecdotes Vimalakirti Second

The "Free Talk" section previously mentioned Gu Zishan of Wuzhong, who built a Yi Garden after retiring from his post. He planted flowers and bamboo and enjoyed poetry and wine. This is true. However, when I was young, I heard my elders say that the funds for building Gu's garden all came from his official pocket when he served as the Ningbo-Shaoxing-Taizhou circuit intendant in Zhejiang. Therefore, after the garden was completed, a humorist saw its inscription and ridiculed it, saying, "He never forgets Ningbo, Shaoxing, and Taizhou!" This is because the character "Yi" (怡) can be broken down into the characters "heart" (心) and "Tai" (台). It can be said that it was a cruel joke.

During the Tongzhi and Guangxu eras, Grand Academician Pan Shunzhi served as the head of the Ziyang Academy in Suzhou for several decades. No headmaster before or after him lasted as long. However, Pan had strong biases when grading papers. The top-ranked students were all famous scholars with good writing skills, while the others were placed there because they were his relatives and old friends. However, there were a few impoverished scholars among the specially ranked students, but they were in the minority. There was a certain student who always received low grades on every exam and had accumulated resentment for a long time. One year, it happened to be Pan's seventieth birthday, so he prepared a self-congratulatory poem and widely solicited students to write matching poems. The original poem was printed and distributed with the exam papers, and the accounting office was instructed to reward those who submitted matching poems generously. The student waited for Pan to be away and submitted his poem. The accounting office did not dare to open it but paid according to the usual procedure. When Pan returned and opened it, he saw the first two lines: "Pan Shunzhi is seventy years old, it is said that to be old and not die is to be a thief." Although Pan was filled with uncontrollable anger, he could do nothing about it.

After Grand Secretary Lu Fengshi passed the imperial examination, someone said that if Lu entered the cabinet, the Qing Dynasty would surely perish. Later, their words came true. People said that the person who said this had foresight. I say that Lu was uninhibited before he passed the examination and was known as the "Touring the City God in the Streets." He had long been looked down upon by society. Once he became the top scholar in the world, people were bound to be unconvinced. Therefore, they fabricated this saying to ridicule him. I did not expect it to become a prophecy.

European Travel Correspondence (97) Liu Haisu

▲ Pilgrimage to Italy Diary

(3) Ten Days in Rome (20)

June 4th Grand Cathedral of Saint Peter Vatican Papal Palace Sistine Chapel

··· ··· ··· ··· ··· ···

Opposite to it, in the middle, are displayed the galloping horses pulling a chariot. Not only are the galloping movement and posture of the horses accurately depicted, but there is also a continuous surge of energy between the front and hind legs, showing a sense of vibrant life. It is titled Bige or Chariot a deux chevaux. The author's name is unknown. Based on its style, we may as well recognize this as a work from the period when Greek sculpture reached its completion.

There are too many treasures here. It's truly "rarities clog the path, and one is overwhelmed!" I also successively saw thirty or forty pieces of stone of various sizes, either a large head or a fragment of a body. Studying them piece by piece, none of them are not rare treasures. However, there are too many large things here, inevitably overshadowing them. I can only briefly describe them here. Gradually walking into the salle en croix grecque, on the central platform is the Venus stone statue, ten feet tall, meticulously crafted by the famous craftsman Praxiteles. The goddess, with her upper body exposed and her hands pulling at the hem of her garment, is the goddess of love and beauty in Greek mythology. This is Praxiteles' masterpiece. The whole is extremely beautiful, with high breasts, a broad forehead, and green eyes, showing a gentle emotion. The hair uses a rough carving technique to achieve the effect of light in painting. This Venus statue has extremely important significance in the expression of the female nude. It is a beautiful goddess statue with a human touch. Before him, there was not much obvious difference between the nude figures of women and the bodies of men. Starting with him, he fully expressed the unique magic and beauty of the female body, so it became a groundbreaking work.

Only their songs can still be heard by us centuries later. They wielded their hands, using blunt knives to carve rough stones, imbuing them with various extraordinary lives. Glory and greatness are one of the endless, infinite lives. Phidias, who created the Parthenon and the Olympian Zeus, and the many Greek masters mentioned above, such as Myron, Praxiteles, and Lysippos, were, like the rest of the Athenians, citizens of free states and believers in polytheism. They were raised in gymnasiums, wrestling, naked, discussing state affairs and voting in the square. Even the most important points in their outlook on life were the same as those of the Greeks of the same era. Their lofty sentiments, elegant faces, and great discoveries and creations were by no means accidental.

The deadline for collection is approaching day by day, and it is necessary to expedite the conclusion. As a result, exchange funds and foreign shipments from various cities have arrived one after another, but the total amount of loans released by the silver and money industry is huge. According to current estimates, only 30% to 40% has been collected, and the majority of the arrears are still outstanding. It is hoped that there will be good results this week, otherwise, silver-deficient families will be affected.

The Stable and Leisurely Flour and Wheat Market

▲ Flour Trading Suspended for Ten Days Starting from the 11th

▲ Wheat Flour: Yesterday, the flour market showed signs of stabilization again. Although the quoted prices for foreign wheat fluctuated, for some reason, the demand from domestic merchants was surprisingly strong. While factories continued to order foreign wheat, they also continued to sell. Because the market sentiment was still firm yesterday, sales were slow, so the market sentiment inevitably appeared bullish. However, the biggest factor was that the opening of this month’s trading period was only for four days. It is said that the market will be closed for ten days from the 11th to the 20th for market repairs, so most speculators are eager to cover their positions, which is also a factor contributing to the improvement of the market. As a result, the price for this month remained unchanged, March increased by one cent, April and May increased by 7.5 li, and June and July increased by 5 li.

▲ Wheat: Yesterday, the futures wheat market generally showed a hovering trend. Since there were no significant fluctuations in foreign wheat, and speculators had already closed their positions, and there was no news of further foreign wheat orders, sellers were rare. On the buying side, because factories remained unchanged, and outsiders gradually reduced their positions due to habit, transactions were very rare. As a result, the prices for this month and March/April remained unchanged, May decreased by one cent, June increased by two cents, and July remained unchanged.

Sugar Market: Coarse and White Sugar Prices Called for Increases, But Demand Was Quiet

Yesterday, the sugar market received telegrams from production areas stating that the spot price of Cuban sugar remained unchanged. In New York, the March price fell by more than two cents, and the prices for other months also fell by one cent each. The spot and futures prices of Java sugar remained weak. Although the market sentiment for No. 24 Dutch coarse and white sugar in the Association market was strong, transactions were few. The asking price increased by ten taels and eight qian, but there were no inquiries. The market was slightly flat. Transactions for medium-grade white sugar were also scarce. The import and export of Japanese sugar were also sporadic, mainly because the closing period was near. N Mark was at ten taels, seven qian and five fen, Meiji YP Mark was at ten taels and nine qian, Minghua goods were at ten taels, eight qian and five fen, YT Mark was at ten taels and seven qian, and YRO Mark was at ten taels and three qian, with slightly more transactions. The rest of the market was unusually quiet.

Piece Goods and Fine Cloth Rise Most Sharply

▲ Tianjin Merchants Still Searching for Goods

▲ Local Factory Cloth: The market continues to rise, especially for fine cloth, which is rising the most sharply. Yesterday, Tianjin merchants made large-scale purchases, causing the price to rise by another one qian to one qian and a half. Trumpet Boy Yang Crane small packages have reached seven taels, and Blue Double Fish has reached seven taels and two qian or so. Fine twill has also risen by one qian. Blue Double Fish is at seven taels and five fen, and Yang Crane is at seven taels and three qian. There is a severe shortage of coarse cloth in stock. Because the price has not yet been announced since the implementation of the factory exit tax, those who had advanced money previously could not export, so both 13-pound and 11-pound goods were in short supply yesterday. However, there is still a large inventory of white flannel. It is currently the off-season, and there have been quite a few sales in recent days, with prices falling by about two qian compared to before.

▲ Eastern and Western Piece Goods: Gold prices are soaring, and everyone is unanimously optimistic. Tianjin merchants were still actively purchasing Eastern goods yesterday. Straight tribute satin, straight tribute woolen cloth, and fine serge were being searched for extensively. Civilized Nankeen and White Crepe, Red Label, which are not yet at the sales season, have also begun to be traded. At this time, when businesses are closing accounts for the Lunar New Year, this large amount of trading is unexpected. Six-pound Guo Ju red cloth sold for four taels and nine qian and a half. Dahe Trading has already opened at five taels. Boy Music Civilized Nankeen was at two qian, three fen, and two and a half li. Man and Dog Crepe was at four taels and two qian and a half. Traders’ asking prices jumped wildly. Santan Straight Tribute Woolen Cloth required four qian and two fen, Ancient City Association Serge required three qian and nine fen, Happiness required three qian, five fen and a half, and Double Boy Deer Straight Tribute Woolen Cloth sold to Tianjin merchants for three qian and four fen. As of yesterday, Yoshida had already opened at three qian and six fen and a half. The intensity of the rise is even greater than before.
